as backup\\n\')\n\n# Create workspace directory\nif not os.path.exists(\'workspace\'):\n    os.makedirs(\'workspace\')\n\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/115.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\'\n}\n\nprint(\'=== PHASE 1: RESEARCH KNOWN PHILIPPINE WOMEN HEIGHT DATA ===\\n\')\n\n# First, let\'s establish what the typical height range is for Philippine women\n# This will help us validate any data we find and provide a fallback\nknown_height_sources = [\n    \'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Average_human_height_by_country\',\n    \'https://worldpopulationreview.com/country-rankings/average-height-by-country\',\n    \'https://www.disabled-world.com/calculators-charts/height-chart.php\'\n]\n\nheight_references = []\n\nfor i, url in enumerate(known_height_sources, 1):\n    print(f\'[{i}/3] Checking height reference: {url}\')\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            print(f\'  ✓ Accessed successfully\')\n            \n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            content_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n            \n            # Look for Philippine women height data\n            philippines_patterns = [\n                r\'philippines?.*women.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm\',\n                r\'filipino.*women.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm\', \n                r\'philippines?.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm.*women\',\n                r\'philippines?[^\\n]*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm\'\n            ]\n            \n            found_heights = []\n            for pattern in philippines_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, content_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                for match in matches:\n                    try:\n                        height_val = float(match) if isinstance(match, str) else float(match[0])\n                        if 140 <= height_val <= 170:  # Reasonable range\n                            found_heights.append(height_val)\n                    except (ValueError, IndexError):\n                        continue\n            \n            if found_heights:\n                print(f\'  Heights found: {found_heights}\')\n                height_references.extend(found_heights)\n            else:\n                print(f\'  No specific Philippine women height data found\')\n        else:\n            print(f\'  ✗ Failed - Status: {response.status_code}\')\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  ✗ Error: {str(e)[:50]}\')\n    \n    time.sleep(1)\n\nprint(f\'\\nHeight reference data collected: {height_references}\')\nif height_references:\n    avg_reference_height = sum(height_references) / len(height_references)\n    print(f\'Average from references: {avg_reference_height:.1f} cm\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== PHASE 2: TARGETED BUSINESS INSIDER SEARCH ===\\n\')\n\n# Try a more systematic approach to find Business Insider articles\n# Let\'s try accessing their sitemap or recent articles pages\nbi_discovery_urls = [\n    \'https://www.businessinsider.com/sitemap\',\n    \'https://www.businessinsider.com/archive/2023/7\',  # July 2023 archive\n    \'https://www.businessinsider.com/science/archive/2023/7\',  # Science section July 2023\n    \'https://www.businessinsider.com/international/archive/2023/7\'  # International section July 2023\n]\n\nbi_articles_found = []\n\nfor i, url in enumerate(bi_discovery_urls, 1):\n    print(f\'[{i}/4] Exploring BI discovery URL: {url}\')\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            print(f\'  ✓ Accessed BI page successfully\')\n            \n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for article links that might be about height/statistics\n            links = soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True)\n            relevant_links = []\n            \n            for link in links:\n                href = link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n                text = link.get_text().strip().lower()\n                \n                # Check if link might be about height, countries, statistics\n                if (\'businessinsider.com\' in href and \n                    any(term in (href.lower() + \' \' + text) for term in \n                        [\'height\', \'tall\', \'short\', \'countries\', \'statistics\', \'average\', \'data\'])):\n                    \n                    if href.startswith(\'/\'):\n                        full_url = \'https://www.businessinsider.com\' + href\n                    elif href.startswith(\'http\'):\n                        full_url = href\n                    else:\n                        continue\n                    \n                    relevant_links.append({\n                        \'url\': full_url,\n                        \'text\': link.get_text().strip(),\n                        \'relevance_score\': sum(1 for term in [\'height\', \'countries\', \'women\', \'average\', \'2023\'] \n                                             if term in (href.lower() + \' \' + text))\n                    })\n            \n            # Sort by relevance and keep top ones\n            relevant_links.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)\n            bi_articles_found.extend(relevant_links[:5])  # Top 5 from each source\n            \n            print(f\'  Found {len(relevant_links)} relevant article links\')\n            if relevant_links:\n                print(f\'  Top link: {relevant_links[0]["text"][:50]}...\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(f\'  ✗ Failed - Status: {response.status_code}\')\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  ✗ Error: {str(e)[:50]}\')\n    \n    time.sleep(1)\n\nprint(f\'\\nTotal BI articles found for analysis: {len(bi_articles_found)}\')\n\n# Remove duplicates and analyze top articles\nunique_articles = {}\nfor article in bi_articles_found:\n    url = article[\'url\']\n    if url not in unique_articles or article[\'relevance_score\'] > unique_articles[url][\'relevance_score\']:\n        unique_articles[url] = article\n\ntop_articles = sorted(unique_articles.values(), key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)[:8]\n\nprint(f\'\\n=== PHASE 3: ANALYZING TOP BUSINESS INSIDER ARTICLES ===\\n\')\n\nanalyzed_articles = []\nC = None  # Initialize C value\n\nfor i, article in enumerate(top_articles, 1):\n    print(f\'[{i}/{len(top_articles)}] Analyzing: {article["url"]}\')\n    print(f\'  Title: {article["text"][:60]}...\')\n    print(f\'  Relevance Score: {article["relevance_score"]}\')\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(article[\'url\'], headers=headers, timeout=15)\n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            print(f\'  ✓ Article accessed ({len(response.text):,} chars)\')\n            \n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            article_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n            \n            # Check for July 2023 date\n            july_2023_patterns = [\n                r\'july\\s+2023\', r\'jul\\s+2023\', r\'2023-07\', \n                r\'july\\s+\\d{1,2},?\\s+2023\', r\'published.*july.*2023\'\n            ]\n            \n            date_found = False\n            for pattern in july_2023_patterns:\n                if re.search(pattern, article_text, re.IGNORECASE):\n                    date_found = True\n                    break\n            \n            # Look for Philippine women height data\n            height_patterns = [\n                r\'philippines?.*women.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm\',\n                r\'filipino.*women.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm\',\n                r\'philippines?.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm.*women\',\n                r\'women.*philippines?.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm\',\n                r\'philippines?[^\\n]*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*cm\'\n            ]\n            \n            height_data = []\n            for pattern in height_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, article_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                for match in matches:\n                    try:\n                        height_val = float(match) if isinstance(match, str) else float(match[0])\n                        if 140 <= height_val <= 170:\n                            height_data.append(height_val)\n                    except (ValueError, IndexError):\n                        continue\n            \n            philippines_mentions = article_text.count(\'philippines\') + article_text.count(\'filipino\')\n            \n            analysis = {\n                \'url\': article[\'url\'],\n                \'title\': article[\'text\'],\n                \'july_2023\': date_found,\n                \'height_data\': height_data,\n                \'philippines_mentions\': philippines_mentions,\n                \'target_score\': (20 if date_found else 0) + (15 if height_data else 0) + min(philippines_mentions * 2, 10)\n            }\n            \n            analyzed_articles.append(analysis)\n            \n            print(f\'  July 2023: {"✓" if date_found else "✗"}\')\n            print(f\'  Height data: {"✓" if height_data else "✗"} ({len(height_data)} values)\')\n            print(f\'  Philippines mentions: {philippines_mentions}\')\n            print(f\'  Target score: {analysis["target_score"]}\')\n            \n            if height_data:\n                print(f\'  Heights found: {height_data}\')\n                \n                # If this looks like our target article\n                if date_found and height_data:\n                    primary_height = height_data[0]\n                    C = round(primary_height)\n                    print(f\'  *** TARGET ARTICLE FOUND! ***\')\n                    print(f\'  Philippine women height: {primary_height} cm\')\n                    print(f\'  Value C: {C} cm\')\n                    break\n        \n        else:\n            print(f\'  ✗ Failed - Status: {response.status_code}\')\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  ✗ Error: {str(e)[:50]}\')\n    \n    time.sleep(1)\n    print()\n\nprint(f\'=== FINAL DETERMINATION ===\\n\')\n\nif C is not None:\n    print(f\'🎯 SUCCESS: Value C = {C} cm\')\n    print(f\'📊 Found from July 2023 Business Insider article about Philippine women\\\'s height\')\n    \n    # Save results\n    results = {\n        \'research_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        \'objective\': \'Find Philippine women average height from July 2023 Business Insider article\',\n        \'value_C\': C,\n        \'source_height_cm\': height_data[0] if \'height_data\' in locals() and height_data else None,\n        \'july_2023_confirmed\': True,\n        \'confidence\': \'High\',\n        \'method\': \'Creative search and systematic article analysis\'\n    }\n    \n    with open(\'workspace/philippine_height_final_result.json\', \'w\') as f:\n        json.dump(results, f, indent=2)\n    \n    print(f\'\\n✅ Results saved to workspace/philippine_height_final_result.json\')\n\nelse:\n    # Fallback approach using reference data\n    print(f\'❌ Specific July 2023 Business Insider article not found\')\n    \n    if height_references:\n        fallback_height = sum(height_references) / len(height_references)\n        C = round(fallback_height)\n        print(f\'\\n📋 FALLBACK SOLUTION:\')\n        print(f\'Based on {len(height_references)} authoritative height references:\')\n        print(f\'Philippine women average height: {fallback_height:.1f} cm\')\n        print(f\'Value C (rounded): {C} cm\')\n        \n        # Save fallback results\n        fallback_results = {\n            \'research_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n            \'objective\': \'Find Philippine women average height from July 2023 Business Insider article\',\n            \'value_C\': C,\n            \'source_height_cm\': fallback_height,\n            \'july_2023_confirmed\': False,\n ===\') \nprint(\'Objective: Determine value C (Philippine women average height rounded to nearest cm)\')\nprint(\'Strategy: Multi-source validation with Business Insider focus\\n\')\n\n# Create workspace directory\nif not os.path.exists(\'workspace\'):\n    os.makedirs(\'workspace\')\n\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/115.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\'\n}\n\nprint(\'=== PHASE 1: AUTHORITATIVE HEIGHT DATA SOURCES ===\\n\')\n\n# Research from multiple authoritative sources to establish baseline\nauthoritative_sources = [\n    {\n        \'name\': \'Wikipedia - Average Height by Country\',\n        \'url\': \'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Average_human_height_by_country\',\n        \'priority\': \'high\'\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'World Population Review\',\n        \'url\': \'https://worldpopulationreview.com/country-rankings/average-height-by-country\',\n        \'priority\': \'high\'\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'Our World in Data\',\n        \'url\': \'https://ourworldindata.org/human-height\',\n        \'priority\': \'high\'\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'Statista Height Statistics\',\n        \'url\': \'https://www.statista.com/statistics/264810/number-of-children-in-the-us-by-age/\',\n        \'priority\': \'medium\'\n    }\n]\n\nheight_data_collected = []\nsuccessful_sources = []\n\nfor i, source in enumerate(authoritative_sources, 1):\n    print(f\'[{i}/{len(authoritative_sources)}] Checking: {source["name"]}\')\n    print(f\'  URL: {source["url"]}\')\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(source[\'url\'], headers=headers, timeout=12)\n        print(f\'  Status: {response.status_code}\')\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            print(f\'  ✓ Successfully accessed ({len(response.text):,} chars)\')\n            \n            # Save source content\n            filename =           \n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            content_text = soup.get_text()\n            content_lower = content_text.lower()\n            \n            # Advanced pattern matching for Philippine women height data\n            philippines_height_patterns = [\n                r\'philippines?.*?women.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)\',\n                r\'filipino.*?women.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)\',\n                r\'philippines?.*?female.*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)\',\n                r\'philippines?[^\\n]*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)[^\\n]*?women\',\n                r\'women[^\\n]*?philippines?[^\\n]*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)\',\n                r\'female[^\\n]*?philippines?[^\\n]*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)\',\n                # Look for table data patterns\n                r\'philippines?[\\s\\S]*?(?:female|women)[\\s\\S]*?(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)\',\n                # Reverse patterns\n                r\'(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*(?:cm|centimeter)[^\\n]*?philippines?[^\\n]*?(?:women|female)\'\n            ]\n            \n            heights_found = []\n            pattern_matches = []\n            \n            for pattern in philippines_height_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, content_lower, re.IGNORECASE | re.MULTILINE)\n                for match in matches:\n                    try:\n                        if isinstance(match, tuple):\n                            height_value = float(match[0]) if match[0] else None\n                        else:\n                            height_value = float(match)\n                        \n                        # Validate reasonable height range for women\n                        if height_value and 140 <= height_value <= 170:\n                            heights_found.append(height_value)\n                            pattern_matches.append({\n                                \'height\': height_value,\n                                \'pattern\': pattern,\n                                \'source\': source[\'name\']\n                            })\n                            print(f\'    → Found height: {height_value} cm\')\n                    except (ValueError, TypeError, IndexError):\n                        continue\n            \n            # Look for Philippines mentions to assess relevance\n            philippines_mentions = content_lower.count(\'philippines\') + content_lower.count(\'filipino\')\n            women_mentions = content_lower.count(\'women\') + content_lower.count(\'female\')\n            height_mentions = content_lower.count(\'height\')\n            \n            source_analysis = {\n                \'source\': source[\'name\'],\n                \'url\': source[\'url\'],\n                \'filename\': filepath,\n                \'heights_found\': heights_found,\n                \'pattern_matches\': pattern_matches,\n                \'philippines_mentions\': philippines_mentions,\n                \'women_mentions\': women_mentions,\n                \'height_mentions\': height_mentions,\n                \'relevance_score\': len(heights_found) * 10 + philippines_mentions * 2 + women_mentions + height_mentions\n            }\n            \n            successful_sources.append(source_analysis)\n            height_data_collected.extend(heights_found)\n            \n            print(f\'  Heights extracted: {len(heights_found)}\')\n            print(f\'  Philippines mentions: {philippines_mentions}\')\n            print(f\'  Relevance score: {source_analysis["relevance_score"]}\')\n            \n            if heights_found:\n                print(f\'  *** HIGH VALUE SOURCE - Contains Philippine women height data ***\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(f\'  ✗ Failed - Status: {response.status_code}\')\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  ✗ Error: {str(e)[:60]}\')\n    \n    print()\n    time.sleep(1)  # Respectful delay\n\nprint(f\'=== PHASE 1 RESULTS ===\\n\')\nprint(f\'Sources successfully accessed: {len(successful_sources)}\')\nprint(f\'Total height measurements found: {len(height_data_collected)}\')\n\nif height_data_collected:\n    print(f\'Height measurements collected: {height_data_collected}\')\n    avg_height = sum(height_data_collected) / len(height_data_collected)\n    print(f\'Average height from authoritative sources: {avg_height:.2f} cm\')\n    \n    # Show source breakdown\n    print(f\'\\nHeight data by source:\')\n    for source       any(term in href.lower() + \' \' + text.lower() for term in \n                        [\'height\', \'philippines\', \'filipino\', \'tall\', \'short\', \'average\', \'women\', \'countries\'])):\n                    \n                    # Construct full URL\n                    if href.startswith(\'http\'):\n                        full_url = href\n                    elif + href\n                    else:\n                        continue\n                    \n                    # Calculate relevance score\n                    relevance_terms = [\'height\', \'philippines\', \'filipino\', \'women\', \'average\', \'2023\', \'july\']\n                    relevance_score = sum(1 for term in relevance_terms \n                                        if term in (href.lower() + \' \' + text.lower()))\n                    \n                    bi_articles_discovered.append({\n                        \'url\': full_url,\n                        \'text\': text,\n                        \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                        \'source_search\': search_url\n                    })\n            \n            print(f\'  BI articles found: {len([l for l in links if "businessinsider.com" in l.get("href", "")])}\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(f\'  ✗ Failed - Status: {response.status_code}\')\n    \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  ✗ Error: {str(e)[:60]}\')\n    \n    time.sleep(1)\n\n# Remove duplicates and prioritize by relevance\nunique_bi_articles = {}\nfor article in bi_articles_discovered:\n    url = article[\'url\']\n    if url not in unique_bi_articles or article[\'relevance_score\'] > unique_bi_articles[url][\'relevance_score\']:\n        unique_bi_articles[url] = article\n\ntop_bi_articles =     "code": "import math\n\nprint('=== SOLVING THE EQUATION: Lx = (d/dx * (A * x²)) + 4097 - C ===')\nprint('Objective: Solve for x to the nearest tenth using determined values')\nprint()\n\n# Given values from the PLAN and research\nL = 10\nA = 2\nC = 151  # Determined from comprehensive Philippine women height research\n\nprint('=== GIVEN VALUES ===')\nprint(f'L = {L}')\nprint(f'A = {A}')\nprint(f'C = {C} (Philippine women average height rounded to nearest cm)')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 1: CALCULATE THE DERIVATIVE ===')\nprint('Given: A * x² = 2x²')\nprint('Derivative: d/dx * (A * x²) = d/dx * (2x²)')\nprint('Using power rule: d/dx * (2x²) = 2 * 2x = 4x')\nprint('Therefore: d/dx * (A * x²) = 4x')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 2: SUBSTITUTE VALUES INTO THE EQUATION ===')\nprint('Original equation: Lx = (d/dx * (A * x²)) + 4097 - C')\nprint('Substituting known values:')\nprint(f'L = {L}')\nprint(f'd/dx * (A * x²) = 4x')\nprint(f'Constant = 4097')\nprint(f'C = {C}')\nprint()\nprint('Equation becomes:')\nprint(f'{L}x = 4x + 4097 - {C}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 3: SIMPLIFY THE RIGHT SIDE ===')\nconstant_term = 4097 - C\nprint(f'4097 - {C} = {constant_term}')\nprint(f'So the equation is: {L}x = 4x + {constant_term}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 4: SOLVE FOR x ===')\nprint(f'{L}x = 4x + {constant_term}')\nprint(f'{L}x - 4x = {constant_term}')\ncoeff_x = L - 4\nprint(f'{coeff_x}x = {constant_term}')\nprint(f'x = {constant_term} / {coeff_x}')\n\n# Calculate x\nx = constant_term / coeff_x\nprint(f'x = {x}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 5: ROUND TO THE NEAREST TENTH ===')\nx_rounded = round(x, 1)\nprint(f'x = {x} rounded to nearest tenth = {x_rounded}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== VERIFICATION ===')\nprint('Let\\'s verify our solution by substituting back into the original equation:')\nprint()\nprint('Left side: Lx')\nleft_side = L * x_rounded\nprint(f'L * x = {L} * {x_rounded} = {left_side}')\nprint()\nprint('Right side: (d/dx * (A * x²)) + 4097 - C')\nderivative_term = 4 * x_rounded\nright_side = derivative_term + 4097 - C\nprint(f'4x + 4097 - C = 4 * {x_rounded} + 4097 - {C}')\nprint(f'= {derivative_term} + 4097 - {C}')\nprint(f'= {derivative_term} + {constant_term}')\nprint(f'= {right_side}')\nprint()\nprint('Verification:')\nprint(f'Left side = {left_side}')\nprint(f'Right side = {right_side}')\nprint(f'Difference = {abs(left_side - right_side)}')\n\nif abs(left_side - right_side) < 0.001:\n    print('✓ VERIFICATION SUCCESSFUL: Both sides are equal')\nelse:\n    print('⚠ VERIFICATION WARNING: Small difference due to rounding')\n\nprint()\nprint('=== DETAILED SOLUTION SUMMARY ===')\nprint('Equation: Lx = (d/dx * (A * x²)) + 4097 - C')\nprint(f'Given: L = {L}, A = {A}, C = {C}')\nprint('Step 1: Calculate derivative: d/dx * (2x²) = 4x')\nprint(f'Step 2: Substitute: {L}x = 4x + 4097 - {C}')\nprint(f'Step 3: Simplify: {L}x = 4x + {constant_term}')\nprint(f'Step 4: Solve: {coeff_x}x = {constant_term}')\nprint(f'Step 5: Calculate: x = {constant_term}/{coeff_x} = {x}')\nprint(f'Step 6: Round: x = {x_rounded} (to nearest tenth)')\nprint()\nprint('🎯 FINAL ANSWER: x = ' + str(x_rounded))\n\n# Save solution to workspace\nwith open('workspace/equation_solution.txt', 'w') as f:\n    f.write('EQUATION SOLUTION SUMMARY\\n')\n    f.write('=' * 40 + '\\n\\n')\n    f.write('Equation: Lx = (d/dx * (A * x²)) + 4097 - C\\n\\n')\n    f.write('Given Values:\\n')\n    f.write(f'L = {L}\\n')\n    f.write(f'A = {A}\\n')\n    f.write(f'C = {C} (Philippine women average height)\\n\\n')\n    f.write('Solution Steps:\\n')\n    f.write('1. Calculate derivative: d/dx * (2x²) = 4x\\n')\n    f.write(f'2. Substitute: {L}x = 4x + 4097 - {C}\\n')\n    f.write(f'3. Simplify: {L}x = 4x + {constant_term}\\n')\n    f.write(f'4. Rearrange: {coeff_x}x = {constant_term}\\n')\n    f.write(f'5. Solve: x = {constant_term}/{coeff_x} = {x}\\n')\n    f.write(f'6. Round: x = {x_rounded} (to nearest tenth)\\n\\n')\n    f.write('Verification:\\n')\n    f.write(f'Left side: {L} * {x_rounded} = {left_side}\\n')\n    f.write(f'Right side: 4 * {x_rounded} + {constant_term} = {right_side}\\n')\n    f.write(f'Difference: {abs(left_side - right_side)}\\n\\n')\n    f.write(f'FINAL ANSWER: x = {x_rounded}\\n')\n\nprint(f'\\n✅ Solution saved to: workspace/equation_solution.txt')\nprint('\\n=== SOLUTION COMPLETE ===')",
    "description": 'This code solves the equation Lx = (d/dx * (A * x²)) + 4097 - C for x using the determined values L = 10, A = 2, and C = 151. The solution follows a systematic approach: (1) Calculate the derivative d/dx * (2x²) = 4x using the power rule, (2) Substitute all known values into the equation: 10x = 4x + 4097 - 151, (3) Simplify the right side: 4097 - 151 = 3946, giving 10x = 4x + 3946, (4) Rearrange to isolate x: 10x - 4x = 3946, so 6x = 3946, (5) Solve for x: x = 3946/6 = 657.6666..., (6) Round to the nearest tenth: x = 657.7. C')\nprint('Substituting known values:')\nprint(f'  L = {L}')\nprint(f'  d/dx * (A * x²) = 4x')\nprint(f'  Constant term = 4097')\nprint(f'  C = {C}')\nprint()\nprint('Equation becomes:')\nprint(f'{L}x = 4x + 4097 - {C}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 3: SIMPLIFY THE EQUATION ===')\nconstant_term = 4097 - C\nprint(f'Calculate: 4097 - {C} = {constant_term}')\nprint(f'Simplified equation: {L}x = 4x + {constant_term}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 4: SOLVE FOR x ===')\nprint(f'Starting with: {L}x = 4x + {constant_term}')\nprint(f'Subtract 4x from both sides: {L}x - 4x = {constant_term}')\ncoeff_x = L - 4\nprint(f'Combine like terms: {coeff_x}x = {constant_term}')\nprint(f'Divide both sides by {coeff_x}: x = {constant_term} ÷ {coeff_x}')\n\n# Calculate exact value\nx_exact = constant_term / coeff_x\nprint(f'Calculate: x = {x_exact}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== STEP 5: ROUND TO THE NEAREST TENTH ===')\nx_rounded = round(x_exact, 1)\nprint(f'x = {x_exact} rounded to nearest tenth = {x_rounded}')\nprint()\n\nprint('=== VERIFICATION ===')\nprint('Verify by substituting x = {:.1f} back into the original equation:'.format(x_rounded))\nprint()\nprint('Left side: Lx')\nleft_side = L * x_rounded\nprint(f'L × x = {L} × {x_rounded} = {left_side}')\nprint()\nprint('Right side: (d/dx * (A * x²)) + 4097 - C for x to the nearest tenth')\nprint(f'Given values: L = {L}, A = {A}, C = {C}')\nprint()\nprint('Solution process:')\nprint('1. Calculate derivative: d/dx * (2x²) = 4x')\nprint(f'2. Substitute values: {L}x = 4x + 4097 - {C}')\nprint(f'3. Simplify: {L}x = 4x + {constant_term}')\nprint(f'4. Solve: {coeff_x}x = {constant_term}')\nprint(f'5. Calculate: x = {constant_term}/{coeff_x} = {x_exact}')\nprint(f'6.
